These quests log entries (F9) give players information about the game:
Icon Name Description Entries
Map Welcome to World of Warcraft Reforged. This map is an open world RPG. This means that you can do whatever you want to. Complete some of the optional quests, hunt other players or forge alliances. Baradé wishes you a lot of fun while playing. I thank EvilPitlord and DeMoNiKuS for the creation of the original map "World of Warcraft Reborn".
  • Creator: Baradé
  • Please provide feedback.
  • Website: https://wowreforged.org
  • Discord: https://discord.gg/eM34z36
  • Development: https://github.com/tdauth/wowr
Support Support the creator of the map. VIPs are allowed to enter the VIP room and the secret chamber from the beginning. It provides them some bonuses in the game which should not be too unfair but still give them a bit of advantage or at least a visible status in the game. VIPs are usually players who helped to improve the map over time.
  • "-q/-news": Shows news with links and QR codes.
  • Support the project to improve its quality.
  • Support the project with a subscription to become a VIP.
  • "-vips": Lists all VIPs.
  • Unlock exclusive features in the map.
  • VIP status on Discord.
Hero Journey Your hero levels will unlock new features in the map.
  • 5: Abilities available on Theramore.
  • 10: Properties.
  • 15: One Equipment Bag.
  • 20: Mount.
  • 25: Second profession.
  • 30: Bonus races.
  • 35: Divine Golems.
  • 40: Bonus heroes and second equipment bag.
  • 45: Second hero and third profession.
  • 50: Boss heroes.
  • 55: Bonus mounts.
  • 60: Second race and third equipment bag.
  • 65: Third hero and third race.
  • 70: AI for yourself.
  • 75: Void Lord can be chosen as hero who can learn different spells.
  • 75: Advanced chat commands from '-helpvisual' can be used.
  • 75: (all three heroes) All races, professions and chat command '-maxbosslevels' are available.
  • Donating/Reporting bugs: VIP.
Known Issues Unfortunately, this map has some known unfixed issues. If you think you know the cause of an issue or the solution to fix it, please report it on Discord.
  • Long loading time leads to errors for some players.
  • Enchanting does not work for all item abilities due to Warcraft bugs.
  • Goblin Town Hall has a weird light bug pointing to the hero glow.
  • Goblin Tower leads to terrain becoming black sometimes.
  • Line of Sight Blockers do not work for flying units (occlusion height).
  • Researches increasing unit maximum life can lead to negative maximum life and instant unit deaths.
  • Release 2.0 of Warcraft III broke older version before 3.31 with a new frame hierarchy.
  • AI might crash in start locations which have too little ground area space.
  • Loading save games might crash because of string literals longer than 1023 characters.
Factions Factions consist of multiple races which allied for a common goal. The two game lobby teams represent the two major factions Alliance and Horde. Players from the same faction are allied by default. The faction The Burning Legion fights against all players. The faction Rescuable allows rescuing respawning units.
  • Alliance
  • Horde
  • The Burning Legion
  • Bosses
  • Rescuable
  • Races belong to one faction or are neutral.
Game Modes You can choose one of two game modes after the hero selection. As a warlord you play partly in the strategy mode and can build a base. This has the advantage that you have mostly a bigger army than other players. On the other hand, as a freelancer your hero starts with +15 points on all attributes and your hero gets 30% more experience from killing hostile units. Freelancers can see neutral buildings from start.
  • Warlord: Partly strategy mode.
  • Freelancer: Pure RPG mode, begins with +15 attributes and +30 % XP rate.
Players Players own heroes, units, buildings and resources. The number of players is determined in the game lobby. Computer players play with Warcraft's AI. Empty slots will not be playing. Users can leave at any time during a game. Users can also be kicked from games by votes.One single player is the host.The ownership of units can be transfered to other players using spells like Charm or chat commands. Players can use their save codes to to save/load data during a game. There are several fixed Computer players which cannot be changed in the game lobby. Alliances between players are preset by their game lobby team. Alliances can be changed during the game using chat commands.
  • "-players": Lists all players with their names, numbers, teams and colors.
  • X in chat commands for players can be their number, name or color name.
  • "-accounts": Lists all known accounts.
  • "-bans": Lists all banned account names.
  • "-votekick X": Starts a votekick against player X.
  • Fixed Computer player Gaia allows rescuing units.
  • Player The Burning Legion plays with Demon AI at Archimonde's realm.
  • Player Bosses owns all bosses and is allied with all creeps.
  • Player Neutral Hostile owns all creeps and is allied with all bosses.
  • Player Neutral Passive owns all NPCs and neutral buildings.
Classes Hero classes determine which spells can be learned by a hero. They give the hero certain traits which are useful when combined with other hero classes.
  • Warrior
  • Hunter
  • Paladin
  • Death Knight
  • Rogue
  • Druid
  • Warlock
  • Monk
  • Arcanist
  • Pyromancer
  • Hydromancer
  • Geomancer
  • Aeromancer
  • Necromancer
  • Witch Doctor
  • Tinker
Heroes You have to pick a hero in the beginning of the game which can be repicked. You are allowed to pick two additional heroes at some point when you reached a higher level with your first hero.
  • "-repick": Repick your hero (you lose all units!).
  • "-fullrepick": Lose 3/4 of your XP but repick the game mode.
  • "-h1/-h2/-h3": to (re)pick hero 1/2/3 without losing all units.
  • Maximum level is 75.
  • Additional, bonus and boss heroes require a higher hero level of your first hero.
  • Hero 2 and 3 have no backpack.
  • Hero 2 and 3 have no backpack and no equipment bags.
  • Available at hero level 40.
Professions After choosing your race or game mode, you have to select a profession. The profession allows you to craft items. These items might help your hero or units to become stronger or to restore their stats or to fortify your base. Crafting items costs mana.
  • Craft items.
  • "-p1/-p2/-p3": (Re)pick your professions 1/2/3.
  • Additional professions require a higher hero level of your first hero.
  • Higher hero levels reduce the crafting cooldowns and increases crafted charges.
Races This selection is restricted to warlords. They receive a scepter and tiny town hall of their race which allows them to summon two workers and therefore to build their first base.
  • For Warlords only.
  • "-r1/-r2/-r3": (Re)pick your races 1/2/3.
  • Additional races require a higher hero level of your first hero.
Start Locations The start locations allow you to start the game at some specified area on the map. Some start locations may be occupied by other players including Warlord AI. The Clan Island is restricted to clan members.
Victory Every player can win the game by killing the boss Archimonde if the victory conditions are enabled. The game ends after this. All players who are not allied with the killing player will lose the game.
  • "-victory"/"-novictory": Enables/disables victory conditions.
Chat Commands Enter the chat commands without the double quotes. The leaderboards will appear during certain quests. Note: Even when the quest has been activated, and you turn off the leaderboard, the counts will continue until the quest requirement is accomplished. Also, it turns off/on the leaderboard display only for the player who writes the chat message.
  • "-h/-help": Lists chat commands.
  • "-helpping": Lists ping chat commands.
  • "-helpclan": Lists clan chat commands.
  • "-helpai": Lists AI chat commands.
  • "-helpally": Lists alliance chat commands.
  • "-helpvisual": Lists visual chat commands.
  • "-helpresources": Lists all resources chat commands.
  • "-helpr/-hr": Lists basic resources chat commands.
  • "-helpattributes": Lists attributes chat commands.
  • "-helpsave": Lists savecode chat commands.
  • "-helpfood": Lists food chat commands.
  • "-helptime": Lists time chat commands.
  • "-helpreset": Lists reset chat commands.
  • "-helpcheats": Lists cheat chat commands.
  • "-helpcinematics": Lists cinematics chat commands.
  • "-c/-clear": Clears all screen messages.
  • "-hide/-show": Disables/enables all custom UI elements.
  • "-uion/off": Enables/disables custom UI when clicking on shops.
  • "-uiqueueon/off": Enables/disables UI training queue.
  • "-uiqueueclear": Clears the UI training queue.
  • "-i/-info/-stats X": Shows info about player X (number, color, name).
  • "-x/-revive": Selects your altar to revive your hero.
  • "-d/-discord": Shows the Discord server URL.
  • "-w/-website": Shows the website URL.
  • "-o/-download": Shows the download URL.

  • "-dp/-diplomacy": Allows the host changing diplomacy settings.
  • "-random": Chooses random settings in the player selection.
  • "-start": Starts the game from the player selection.
  • "-rs/-randomstart": Chooses random settings and starts the game from the player selection.
  • "-h1/-h2/-h3": Allows you to (re)pick your heroes keeping their XP.
  • "-p1/-p2/-p3": Allows you to (re)pick your professions only.
  • "-r1/-r2/-r3": Allows you to (re)pick your races only.
  • "-repick": Allows you to choose a new hero but removes all of your units from the map!
  • "-fullrepick": Lose 3/4 of your XP and Evolution but repick the game mode.
  • "-g/-get": Recreates hero profession and race items.
  • "-unlock/-lock": Allows you to unlock everything in the map.
  • "-victory"/"-novictory": Enables/disables victory conditions.
  • "-nostats"/"-stats": Disables/enables stats GUI.
  • "-auto": Auto skills all heroes in selection.
  • "-it/-items": Shows all backpack items.

  • "-zoneson/off": Enables/disables zone info.
  • "-z/-zone": Shows the zone info of your selected unit.
  • "-zf/-zonefull": Shows the full zone info of your selected unit.
  • "-k/-suicide": Kills your selected units.
  • "-anim X": Plays animation X for all selected units.
  • "-transfer ": Allows you to transfer chosen units to an allied player.
  • "-notransfer": Cancels the transfer process.
  • "-players": Shows the numbers of all playing players.
  • "-votekick X": Starts a votekick against player X.
  • "-yes": Votes for a votekick.
  • "-ping": Pings the current quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingh": Pings all allied heroes.

  • "-pingm": Pings all of your mounts.

  • "-crusadeon/-crusadeoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.

  • "-allyvu X": Ally player X with shared vision and units.
  • "-allyvuf X": Ally player X with fully shared vision and units.

  • "-unally X": Unally player X.
  • "-unallyv X": Unally player X with shared vision.

  • "-builder"/"-nobuilder": Creates/removes a builder for player 1 red.

  • "-cheats"/"-nocheats": Enables/disables cheat chat commands.
  • "-train"/"-notrain": Enables/disables the railway on the map.
  • "-resetevolution X": Resets level of research Evolution back to X.
Universal Chat Commands Enter the chat commands without the double quotes. These chat commands are available by Warcraft III: Reforged and in Battle.net.
  • "/help X": Shows usage help for topic X (whisper etc.).
  • "/fps": Shows FPS.
  • "/ping": Shows ping.
  • "/whois X": Shows information about Battle.net user X.
  • "/whoami": Shows information about your Battle.net user.
  • "/w X": Sends a private message to Battle.net user X.
  • "/ignore X": Ignores all future messages from Battle.net user X.
  • "/unignore X": Unignores all future messages from Battle.net user X.
  • "/users": Shows number of users currently on Battle.net.
  • "/time": Shows passed game time.
Cheats Cheats are enabled automatically for player WorldEdit in single player and help testing the map.
  • "-helpcheats": Lists cheat chat commands.
  • "-nocheats/-cheats": Disables/enables cheat chat commands.
  • "-unfreeze: Unfreezes everything.
  • "-nocreeps": Removes all creep units.
  • "-nobosses": Removes all boss units.
  • "-nopassive": Removes all neutral passive units.
  • "-creeps": Lists missing creeps.
  • "-cinoutro": Shows the outro cinematic.
  • "-cinlichking": Shows the Lich King cinematic.
  • "-cinoldgods": Shows the Old Gods cinematic.
  • "-cininvasion": Shows the Invasion cinematic.
  • "-boots": Creates the Boots of Teleportation.
  • "-tool": Creates the Goblin Tool Box.
  • "-spade": Creates a Spade item.
  • "-terrain": Shows the current terrain type.
  • "-heroskills": Shows all wrongfully registered hero skills.
  • "-bonus": Shows the bonus system config.
  • "-quests": Enables Jaina quests and some more.
  • "-fields": Checks registered object data fields.
  • "-read": Checks file reading.
  • "-write": Checks file writing.
  • "-maxresources": Gives you maximum resources of all resources.
  • "-respawngroupcounter": Shows the maximum number of respawn unit groups.
  • "-respawnall": Respawns all dead creep unit groups.
  • "-maxlevel": Sets all heroes to their maximum level.
  • "-level X": Sets the hero level of the selected heroes to X.
  • "-reset": Resets the cooldowns of all selected units.
  • "-medivh": Creates Medivh's Spell Book for your primary hero.
  • "-revive": Instantly revives your primary hero.
  • "-resetrepick": Resets repick cooldowns.
  • "-demigodlight": Makes your primary hero a light Demigod.
  • "-demigoddark": Makes your primary hero a dark Demigod.
  • "-trydemigod": Creates all units and items to become a Demigod.
  • "-orderon": Enables order debug messages.
  • "-orderoff": Disables order debug messages.
  • "-kill": Kills all selected units.
  • "-fill": Fills life and mana of all selected units.
  • "-share": All players share control with you.
  • "-unitinfo": Shows info of all selected units.
  • "-checksave": Checks writing and reading save codes.
  • "-generatesave": Generates some predefined save codes.
  • "-savecounters": Lists all counters for all save code objects.
  • "-savecodeduplicates": Lists all duplicates for all save code objects.
  • "-savecodemissing": Lists all duplicates missing save code objects from all placed map objects.
  • "-combination": Shows the current combination for the Tomb of Sargeras dungeon.
  • "-foldername": Shows the name of the folder for save code files.
  • "-autoskill": Auto skills your first hero and all boss heroes.
  • "-orbs": Creates all orb items for your first hero.
  • "-items": Creates all items for you.
  • "-herolevels": Shows hero levels calculated by XP.
  • "-deathwing": Spawns Death Wing.
  • "-claws": Creates Claws of Attack +15 items for your first hero.
  • "-clawsbonus": Creates items with a Claws of Attack bonus for your first hero.
  • "-regennight": Shows the value of the regeneration type Night.
  • "-craft": Creates Crafting Stashes and recipe and ingredient items at New Stormwind.
  • "-achievementscheat": All time achievement are triggered.
  • "-legendary": Creates all legendary items at the center of your camera.
  • "-professions": Creates all profession items.
  • "-aigui": Shows the AI player settings UI.
  • "-aicraft": Auto crafts for all AI players.
  • "-aiharveston": Enables you the AI gold harvest bonus for you.
  • "-aiharveston": Disables the AI gold harvest bonus for you.
  • "-day": Changes the time of day to 12.
  • "-night": Changes the time of day to 0.
  • "-jaina": Enables the Jaina quest 1.
  • "-arena": Enables the Stonemaul arena.
  • "-evolution X": Sets the level of your Evolution research to X.
  • "-evolutioncreeps X": Sets the level of the creeps Evolution research to X.
  • "-loadmines": Loads mines automatically.
  • "-website": Generates all website data.
Warcraft III Cheats Warcraft III provides a number of cheat codes to test maps. These only work in singleplayer. Press the enter key, type in the code, and press enter again. Cheat codes are not case sensitive.
  • "WhosYourDaddy": God mode. All units and building gains invulnerability and one-shot opponents.
  • "ISeeDeadPeople": Reveal full map and disable fog of war.
  • "SharpAndShiny": Instantly grant all upgrades.
  • "WarpTen": Speeds up construction of buildings and units.
  • "WhoIsJohnGalt": Speeds up research time for upgrades.
  • "Synergy": Disables tech tree requirements.
  • "KeyserSoze X": Gives you X Gold.
  • "LeafitToMe X": Gives you X Lumber.
  • "GreedIsGood X": Gives you X Gold and Lumber.
  • "PointBreak": Disable Food limit.
  • "ThereIsNoSpoon": Unlimited Mana.
  • "TheDudeAbides": Resets all cooldowns.
  • "IocainePowder": Enables fast acting death/decay of bodies.
  • "StrengthAndHonor": Disables game over screen after losing objectives in campaign mode.
  • "ItVexesMe": Disables victory conditions.
  • "Motherland X Y": Level jump for race X to level Y.
  • "SomebodySetUpUsTheBomb": Instant defeat.
  • "AllYourBaseAreBelongToUs": Instant victory.
  • "RiseAndShine": Set time of day to dawn.
  • "LightsOut": Set time of day to dusk.
  • "DayLightSavings X": If a time is specified for X, time of day is set to that, otherwise time of day is alternately halted/resumed.
  • "TenthLevelTaurenChieftain": Plays Power of the Horde by Tenth Level Tauren Chieftain.
Repick You can select your hero again by using the chat command "-repick". He keeps the gained experience but you lose all units on the map! All of your carried items will be dropped on the island Theramore, so quest items and rewards won't get lost. Repicks are allowed only every 30 seconds. You cannot rechoose your initially selected game mode.
  • Use "-repick".
  • Keeps only your XP.
  • You lose all units, buildings and resources.
  • Items will be dropped on Theramore.
  • You cannot change your game mode.
Full Repick You can select your hero again including the game mode by using the chat command "-fullrepick". He keeps only a part of the gained experience and you lose all units on the map! All of your carried items will be dropped on the island Theramore, so quest items and rewards won't get lost. Repicks are allowed only every 30 seconds. You can reselect your initial game mode.
  • Use "-fullrepick".
  • Keeps only 1/4 of your XP.
  • You lose all units, buildings and resources.
  • Items will be dropped on Theramore.
  • You can change your game mode.
Alliances Alliances can be changed via the default Warcraft menu. You can also send resources via the standard menu. There are chat commands for single player games to change the alliances. The AI should react to your alliance changes. When you ally an AI player, the player should ally you as well etc. Special AI players or bosses are not included.
  • "-ffa": Free For All. Every player has his/her own team.
  • "-lobby": Use lobby teams.
  • "-friends": Ally all players.
  • "-friendsv": Ally all players with shared vision.
  • "-friendsvu": Ally all players with shared vision and units.
  • "-friendsvuf": Ally all players with shared vision and fully shared units.
  • "-enemies": Unally all players.
  • "-ally X": Ally player X.
  • "-allyv X": Ally player X with shared vision.
  • "-allyvu X": Ally player X with shared vision and units.
  • "-allyvuf X": Ally player X with fully shared vision and units.
  • "-neutral X": Become neutral to player X.
  • "-neutralv X": Become neutral to player X with shared vision.
  • "-unally X": Unally player X.
  • "-unallyv X": Unally player X with shared vision.
Hero Death If your hero dies you can either revive him/her in your own built altar if you are a warlord or revive him/her in the altar on Theramore or in your hideout. You can leave the island by buying a boat. If you have no gold, just sell crafted items. Note that ressurecting your hero on Theramore takes longer than in your own altar or hideout. Resurrection Stones allow reviving your hero automatically.
  • "-x/-revive": Selects your altar to revive your hero.
  • "-suicide": Kills your selected units.
  • "-noresurrect": Disables all activated Resurrection Stones.
  • "-noresurrectX": Disables the activated Resurrection Stone for hero X.
  • "-pingaltars": Pings all of your altars.
  • "-pingres/resurrectionstones": Pings all resurrection stones.
Cities and Hideouts Every warlord-type Hero has a nation-specific scepter. With this he or she can summon workers who will start building their nations. It is recommended that they build within city walls because the probability of their buildings being attacked by creeps or "terrorist" Heros is considerably lowered. Also, they can spawn citizens and build housings for them. Citizens make your town more realistic and also have some useful abilities. Hideouts are for Freelancer Heros. They are their personal homes and provide among other things a safe place to recover. It should be considered building them within city walls or under the protection of a warlord player to lower destruction probability.
Player Housings Players can purchase their own housings if it has been unlocked for their account. Your own housing is a location for your units to be safe and invite other players. Player housings allow customization.
  • Purchase at the Caretaker at Theramore.
  • Requires to be unlocked for your account name.
  • Neutral safe zone.
  • Allows customization.
  • Invite other players and units.
Resources Resources allow training, buying and upgrading units, constructing buildings, researching upgrades and buying items. Different resources have a different value. More valuable resources are usually harder to harvest.
  • "-helpresources": Lists resources chat commands.
  • "-resources X": Shows the resources of player X or your resources.
  • "-resguion/-resgui": Shows the resource GUI.
  • "-resguioff": Hides the resources GUI.
  • "-sell X Y": Sells the amount Y of resource X for gold.
  • "-sellall": Sells all resources except gold and lumber for gold.
  • "-sellwood": Sells all lumber for gold.
  • "-buy X Y": Buys the amount Y of resource X for gold.
  • "-resinfo/-resourcesinfo": Shows the resource information about the first selected unit.
  • "-loadres X": Loads your resources from savecode X.
Computer AI Computer players are warlords by default. They start with a main building, five workers and their hero. The AI will collect gold and lumber and build additional gold mines. It should attack creeps and hostile players from time to time. If you are allied to a computer player it is recommended to defend him and to give him resources if you are a warlord yourself. Allied computer players might turn out to be rather useful when attacking another player. When the base of a computer player is destroyed, the hero will get a tiny main building to rebuild a base. Their race is defined in the beginning by the host player.
  • Change alliances to get control.
  • "-aireset": Resets the AI players and allows customizing them from the host.
  • "-aion/off X": Turn AI on/off for player X.
  • "-aiignoreall X": Disable AI unit control for player X.
  • "-aiignore": Disable AI unit control for all selected units.
  • "-aiuse": Enable AI unit control for all selected units.
  • "-aiattackson/off X": Turn AI attacks on/off for player X.
  • "-aiattacksplayerson/off X": Turn AI player attacks on/off for player X.
  • "-aishipsson/off X": Turn AI ships on/off for player X.
  • "-aigold/wood X": Ask AI player X for gold/wood.
  • "-aiexpansions X Y": Sets Y expansions for player X.
  • "-aishredders X Y": Sets Y shredders for player X.
  • "-aizeppelins X Y": Sets Y zeppelins for player X.
  • "-aihero X Y Z": Replaces hero Y with Z for player X.
  • "-ailoadmines X": Loads mines for player X.
  • "-airevive X": Revives heroes for player X.
  • "-aiprofession X Y": Changes profession of allied player X to Y.
  • "-aiinfo X": Shows information about player X.
  • "-aitargeton/off X": Enables/disables AI attacking target for player X.
  • "-aitarget X": Sets the AI target for player X to your hero 1 location.
  • "-legion": Enables The Burning Legion.
  • "-nolegion": Disables The Burning Legion.
Creeps You can kill creeps to increase the level of your hero. There is different creeps everywhere in the world. When you kill a group of computer-controlled creeps, it will be respawned after 100 seconds, so the number of opponents in the game is not finite. Some groups leave items after their extermination which can be picked up by your hero. The creeps won't respawn if there is a building in the area. When the building is destroyed, the creeps will respawn again.
Bosses Bosses are marked by the red skulls on the minimap. They are creep heroes which you can kill to gain experience and their legendary item. Each legendary item is unique in the game and has some powerful abilities. The legendary items are reset to their boss location when your first hero dies even if it is placed in your backpack or equipment bag.
  • "-pingbosses/pingb/bosses": Pings all bosses.
Legendary Artifacts Legends and rumors speak of many legendary Artifacts hidden across the World. The bad news is, you can´t get them for free, but in order to retrieve them, must defeat each Dungeon Master guarding them. Since the Artifact Guardians are very powerful, it is advised not to venture alone into their lairs, or at least not well prepared. If a Hero carrying a unique artifact DIES without an Ankh or the Reincarnation skill, the artifacts will be removed from the Hero. They can then again be retrieved from the location where they were originally found.
  • "-pingl": Pings all legendary items which are on the ground.
Quests You can solve optional quests to get items as rewards. You recognize NPCs who give quests by the exclamation mark over their heads. If one player accepts a quest, he/she or any other player can solve the quest and gets a reward from the NPC for it. Use the chat command "-ping" to ping the current quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-ping": Pings the current quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pinghuman": Pings the current Human quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingvillage": Pings the current Village quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingdalaran": Pings the current Dalaran quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingkultiras": Pings the current Kul Tiras quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingnightelf": Pings the current Night Elf quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingorc": Pings the current Orc quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingbloodelf": Pings the current Blood Elf quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingnaga": Pings the current Naga quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingforsaken": Pings the current Forsaken quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pinglichking": Pings the current Lich King quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingdraenei": Pings the current Draenei quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingdemon": Pings the current Demon quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingpanda": Pings the current Pandaren quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingeredar": Pings the current Eredar quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingtuskarr": Pings the current Tuskarr quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pinggoblin": Pings the current Goblin quest locations on the minimap.
  • "-pingjaina": Pings the current Jaina quest locations on the minimap.
Backpack You can select your backpack at the left top corner directly under your hero icon, so your hero can carry enough items with him/her. Use the two abilities in the backpack to change the current bag.
Equipment Bags Equipment bags allow your hero to equip additional items and to skill additional spells.
  • Require a higher hero level of your first hero.
  • Available on Theramore.
  • Limited to 3.
  • 6 additional items per bag.
  • 5 additional spells per bag.
Leaderboards Some epic quests will create leaderboards. In order to hide or show them again, use following commands (works only if the quests are activated): 1. CRUSADE: - turn on leaderboard: "-crusadeon" - turn off leaderboard: "-crusadeoff" 2. THE SILVER HAND: - turn on leaderboard: "-paladinson" - turn off leaderboard: "-paladinsoff" 3. CENTAUR KHANS: - turn on leaderboard: "-centaurson" - turn off leaderboard: "-centaursoff" Note: Even when the quest has been activated, and you turn off the leaderboard, the counts will continue until the quest requirement is accomplished. Also, it turns off/on the leaderboard display only for the player who writes the chat message.
  • "-crusadeon/-crusadeoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-centaurson/-centaursoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-paladinson/-paladinsoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-draeneion/-draeneioff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-demonson/-demonsoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-whaleson/-whalessoff": Enable/disable leaderboard.
  • "-oldgodson/off": Enables/disables leaderboard.
  • "-invasionon/off": Enables/disables leaderboard.
  • "-elementalon/off": Enables/disables leaderboard.
  • "-wildon/off": Enables/disables leaderboard.
Demigod If you are bored with the standard heroes and you want to become more powerful, you can become a demigod. You can do this by buying either a 'Order Stone Fragment' (light side) or a 'Chaos Stone Fragment' (dark side) and by placing your hero in the center of the middle island above the Maelstorm, You have to place a level 10 dragon of the corresponding color in each fire. If your hero uses the item in the center of the island he/she will become a demigod automatically. The hero keeps the gained experience.
  • Order Stone Fragment: Eternal Guardian - Light Demigod
  • Chaos Stone Fragment: Hand of Destruction - Dark Demigod
Mounts When your hero gets to level 20 he/she can cast an ability which summons a flying mount. This mount can transport one unit. Your hero can use it to fly over the Ocean or cliffs to get wherever he/she wants to. Your mount will be different depending on the race of your hero.
  • Summon the Mount at level 20.
  • "-mountname1/2/3 X": Changes the name of the mount to X.
Divine Golems When your hero gets to level 35 you can train powerful Divine Golems.
  • Can be trained at level 35.
  • Cause Chaos damage.
  • Immune to spells.
  • Limited to 8.
Evolution You can research Evolution to increase the the maximum life, damage, armour and level of all of your units, so they will give enemy players more XP. The upgrade is also used for all creeps and units from bosses on the map as soon as the hero of playing users with the lowest hero level hits level 10. The upgrade is useful to continue leveling in late game and to kill strong heroes with a stronger army of units if you invested into units more than leveling.
  • Balances units for higher hero levels.
  • Increases maximum life and damage of all units.
  • Increases the level and armor every 10 levels.
  • Does not affect buildings.
  • Used for creeps and boss units every 10 hero levels at once.
  • Creep level determined by the lowest hero level of playing users.
Goblin Bank The Goblin Bank is a neutral building located Theramore. You can use it to increase your gold and lumber by depositing it for some time and getting interests. You can also play the Wheel of Fortune there.
  • Deposit gold and lumber to get interests.
  • 5.0 % interest rate.
  • Win gold, lumber or units with Wheel of Fortune.
  • "-goblindeposit": Shows your gold and lumber in the Goblin Bank.
Clans You can either create or join a clan. Clans are groups of players who want to play together. Clans have members, a name, one leader, several captains and store gold and lumber for all members. Clans can have one Clan Hall in a game. Their stats will be stored in savecodes which can be improved even when not all clan members are playing.
  • "-loadc XXX": Loads the clan savecode XXX.
  • "-clanspresave": Lists the prestored clan savecodes.
  • "-loadclanp X": Loads the prestored clan savecode X.
  • "-clanrename X": Renames your clan to X.
  • "-clangold X": Deposits X gold.
  • "-clanlumber X": Deposits X lumber.
  • "-clanwgold X": Withdraws X gold.
  • "-clanwlumber X": Withdraws X lumber.
  • "-clans": Shows a list of all playing clans.
  • "-claninfo": Shows info about your clan.
  • "-clanrank X Y": Sets the rank of player X to Y.
  • "-claninvite X": Invites player X to join your clan.
  • "-clanaccept": Accepts a clan invitation.
  • "-clanleave": Leave your current clan.
  • "-clanaion/off": Enables/disables resource messages from AI players.
  • Change the clan icon at the Clan Meeting Point.
Reward Freelancers Warlords can reward freelancers with an ability in their main building. This will give a freelancer 800 gold, 800 lumber and 200 experience. It can be done every 180 seconds and helps to push freelancers.
Transfer Units Every player can give units to an allied player with an ability in his/her base or hideout. After using the ability on the given units you have to enter "-give playernumber" to give the units to a certain player. You can enter "-nogive" to cancel the process or simply cast the ability again.
Stonemaul Gauntlet The Stonemaul Ogres are famous for their passion for combat and fighting games. Their new warchief Rexxar has inspired them to establish a public gladiator arena. Here Heros can choose between different opponents to fight against in order to gain experience and maybe some small rewards. However, the Arena must first be officially opened by a certain Orc Quest. If you choose to fight in the arena, there is no turning back. If you enter the Arena with more than 1 Hero (Hero group), you lose the contest as soon as the 1st Hero dies. And if a Hero leaves the Arena before the fight is over, the battle is also over and you prove your cowardness to the Stonemaul Ogres. Aaahahahaharrr!
Car Races The Goblins on Kezan provide races which let the winners earn valuable cups. You have to buy a qualification to start a race. There can be only one race at a time. The first three winners will get a cup which can be sold. You can only participate with your first hero. Move your hero to all check points of the race in the correct order in the given time to win it.
  • Buy a qualification on Kezan to start.
  • Participate with your first hero.
Railway The Gnomish railway moves around Azeroth on the sea and land tracks. It allows any unit to enter or leave the train at railway stations which are around Azeroth. Units in the train are protected. The train can move in both directions.
  • "-train"/"-notrain": Enables/disables the railway on the map.
Marketplaces Marketplaces sell items dropped by creeps.
  • Sells dropped items.
  • Exists on Theramore for all players.
  • Can be built by Female Citizens.
  • Limited to 1 per player.
Thieve Guilds Thieves Guilds sell units of enemy killed unit types. If you kill creeps or enemy units, your Thieve Guild will sell the unit. It is limited to only 1 to keep it balanced.
  • Sells killed creeps.
  • Exists on Theramore for all players.
  • Can be built by Female Citizens.
  • Limited to 1 per player.
Trading Posts Trading Posts allow buying and selling resources.
  • Allow buying and selling resources.
Properties Properties are unique indestructible buildings at fixed locations which can be purchased by one single player during the game. They allow hiring race-specific units and gathering resources by loading workers.
  • "-pingproperties": Pings all properties.
  • Unique places.
  • Hire units and get all researches from one race.
  • Gather one specific resource by loading workers.
  • Produce food.
Player Stats There is a multiboard at the top right of the screen with the title "Stats" to show player stats of all players. It might help you to identify strong/weak players and compare yourself to other players. The counter in the header shows how many human players are still online from the beginning of the game. It does not include AI players or unused slots. It also shows the elapsed time of the game. Every row has the color of the player to make it easier to find the values of a certain player.
  • Stats X/Y: online/total human players.
  • X:Y:Z - Elapsed game time in hours, minutes and seconds.
  • Player number, player name
  • Team
  • Clan
  • 1. Race
  • 2. Race
  • 3. Race
  • 1. Profession
  • 2. Profession
  • 3. Profession
  • 1. Hero Level
  • 2. Hero Level
  • 3. Hero Level
  • Gold
  • Lumber
  • Food
  • Evolution Level
Special Race Buildings Every race has a special building which can be researched in the Tier 3 town hall and built by the Male Citizen. It can only be built once and has some special abilities for the race which have their origin in the lore of Warcraft III.
  • Require Tier 3 Town Hall.
  • Require a unique research from Tier 3.
  • Limited to 1.
Save Codes You can save/load your hero settings and XP. However, it is restricted to the corresponding game type since the game type influences how fast you gain XP etc. Just make a screenshot of the savecode to store it on your disk.
  • "-savecodeconverter": Allows you converting old savecodes into new ones.
  • "-presave": Lists the prestored savecodes.
  • "-clanspresave": Lists the prestored clan savecodes.
  • "-loadp X": Loads the prestored savecode X.
  • "-loadclanp X": Loads the prestored clan savecode X.
  • "-save": Saves your hero and prints the savecode.
  • "-savec": Saves your hero without info.
  • "-saveautoon": Enables auto saving of your hero.
  • "-saveautooff": Disables auto saving of your hero.
  • "-load XXX": Loads your hero from savecode XXX.
  • "-saveautoon/off": Enables/disables auto saving of your hero.
  • "-savegui": Shows the GUI for savecodes.
  • "-asave": Saves all savecodes in the auto load file.
  • "-aload": Loads all save codes from the auto load file.
  • "-areset": Allows saving and loading automatic save codes.
  • Requires matching player name and game mode etc.
  • Savecodes are stored in "C:\\Users\\XXX\\Documents\\Warcraft III\\CustomMapData".
  • Press the Print key to store a screenshot.
  • Screenshots stored in "C:\\Users\\XXX\\Documents\\Warcraft III\\ScreenShots".
  • "-loadi XXX": Loads items from savecode XXX.
  • "-loadu XXX": Loads units from savecode.
  • "-loadb XXX": Loads buildings from savecode.
  • "-loadr X": Loads your researches from savecode X.
  • "-loadres X": Loads your resources from savecode X.
  • "-loadc XXX": Loads the clan savecode XXX.
  • "-loadl XXX": Loads the letter savecode XXX.
  • "-savecheck XXX": Checks savecode XXX.
  • "-generated": Lists all generated savecodes from the current game.
  • "-cleargenerated": Clears all generated savecodes from the current game.
  • Legendary items and quest rewards are not saved.
  • Race and Freelancer units/buildings must match your mode.
Portals The whole map contains many portals connecting places with each other. This is required to allow the AI to get everywhere easily without buying Zeppelins but also to connect all players with each other. No player should have an unfair advantage of reaching places much faster than others. Portals can also be built by Citizens to connect your different bases with each other. You won't have to cross the whole map with your army to defend your other bases. A research allows your built portals to teleport your units to any discovered place on the map except it is protected by an Antimagic Ward.
  • Male citizens can build Portals.
  • Connect bases with each other.
  • Teleport your army to any discovered area.
  • Exist for ships on the sea.
  • "-portals"/"-noportals": Enables/disables neutral portals.
Crafting Stashes Crafting Stashes can be built by male citizens and allow you to craft items and summon creatures given the required items. Put the required items in the inventory and craft or summon as many items or creatures as you want to. Link Crafting Stashes with each other, to use multiple inventories for required items.
  • Allow crafting items.
  • Allow summoning creatures.
  • Required items for recipes must be placed in their inventory.
  • Can be built by male citizens.
Mounts Cages Mounts Cages allow your hero to change his/her mount. Different mounts have different abilities, movement speeds and types.
  • Allow changing the mount for heroes.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
Dragon Roosts Dragon Roosts allow you to train all different types of dragons.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
  • Limited to 1.
  • Require a research from housings.
Antimagic Wards Antimagic Wards can be built by female citizens. They block the enemy sight for the area around them. They also block enemy teleportation spells for this area and allow silencing enemy units.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
  • Limited to 1.
Spell Books Spell Books can be built by female citizens. They contain all learnable hero spells. Only reskillable heroes can learn them.
  • Allow changing hero spells for customizable heroes and equipment bags.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
Alchemist Labs Alchemist Labs can be built by female citizens. They allow converting units into different races.
  • Convert units into different races.
  • Require hero level 75.
  • Require tier 3.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
Hero Abilities Hero Abilities can be built by female citizens. They your heroes to change their standard abilities.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
  • Change standard hero abilities.
Witch Huts Witch Huts can be built by female citizens. They allow giving units different abilities. The units are permanently stored for mounts.
  • Can be built by female citizens.
  • Give units different abilities.
  • Require hero level 75.
  • Require tier 3.
  • Abilities are stored for mounts.
Armories Armories can be built to buy equipment items for customizable heroes.
  • Can be built by children.
  • Equipment items for customizable heroes.
Void Lords You can pick the Void Lord as hero when your main hero has reached the maximum hero level. The Void Lord can reskill all of his hero spells at the Arcane Academy of Theramore. Every spell slot can have one of several given hero spells. Once you have learned a hero spell, you can reset all hero spells to reskill again. There is a version of this special hero for every primary attribute. The hero causes Chaos damage and can walk on water.
  • Require maximum hero level.
  • Spells can be customized.
  • Cause Chaos damage.
  • Can walk on water.
Customizable Heroes Customizable heroes can change their hero attributes, spells and skins.
  • "-helpattributes": Lists attributes chat commands.
  • "-str X": Skills X strength. Skills max strength if empty.
  • "-agi X": Skills X agility. Skills max agility if empty.
  • "-int X": Skills X intelligence. Skills max intelligence if empty.
  • "-reseta": Resets attributes.
  • "-equala": Equally skilled attributes.
  • "-rename X": Renames selected heroes into X.
  • Female Citizens can build Attributes.
  • Female Citizens can build Hero Abilities.
Rescuable Units owned by player Rescuable can be rescued by any other player. Rescued units change their owner to the rescuing player. Rescuing units is only possible if you the player has enough food left to rescue the unit.
  • Units owned by Rescuable can be rescued when approaching them.
  • Approach them with units by a playing user.
  • Change owner to the rescuing player.
  • Respawn automatically like creeps.
  • Require enough unused food.
Lore The lore in this map is based on everything in the original map World of Warcraft Reborn which seems to be World of Warcraft Classic. The additional stuff from the Reforged version is mostly based on the Warcraft III campaigns and not World of Warcraft or any of its expansions since I have never really played World of Warcraft and the lore seems to be too much to know everything. I took most information from the campaign missions of the Reign of Chaos and Frozen Throne campaigns, so do not be disappointed if there is lots of stuff missing which exists in or different from World of Warcraft.
Baradé
  • Original lore from Reborn based on WoW Classic.
  • Additional lore based on the Warcraft III campaigns.
  • Does not follow the WoW Expansions.
Tomes Tomes are items which increase hero stats permanently. Hence, they are disabled by default to keep the game balanced. However, they can be enabled by a vote. This allows buying and crafting tomes as well as loading them via save codes.
  • Items which increase hero stats permanently.
  • "-tomes"/"-notomes": Enables/disables tomes.
  • Can only be loaded with save codes if enabled.
  • Available in the Library at Theramore.
  • Profession Scribe allows crafting tomes.
Cinematics Cinematics can be disabled.
  • Shown to all players at the same time.
  • "-helpcinematics": Lists cinematics chat commands.
  • "-cinematics"/"-nocinematics": Enables/disables cinematics.
  • "-cindalaran": Plays the cinematic Dalaran.
Achievements Achievements can be gained by increasing the games progress, killing units etc. They will give players an XP bonus, items, resources etc. and might be a motivation to do stuff in the map.
  • "-achievements": Lists all available achievements with your score.
  • Conqueror: 7000 XP for constructing a town hall in every start location.
  • Quest Solver: 100 XP * all completed quests every %2% completed quests by any player.
  • Master Quest Solver: 6000 XP for completing all quests.
  • Boss Slayer: 100 XP * all different killed bosses every 5 killed bosses.
  • Master Boss Slayer: 5000 XP for killing every boss.
  • Creep Slayer: 2 XP * 50 creeps of the same type every 50 killed creeps.
  • Master Creep Slayer: 5000 XP for killing a creep of every type.
  • Hero Slayer: 10 XP * all killed enemy heroes every enemy hero kill.
  • Player Slayer: 200 XP per defeated player.
  • Deforestation: 5000 XP per defeated player.
  • Without Friends: 1000 XP * 2/4/6/8/10 hours straight.
  • Overpopulation: 1500 XP for 600 food used.
  • Demon Hunter: 10000 XP for killing Archimonde within 30 minutes.
  • Master Locksmith: 1000 XP per 50 unlocked chests.
  • Master Thief: 1000 XP per 50 stolen items.
  • Survivor: 2000 XP for 2 hours without your hero dying.
  • Holy Warrior: 1000 XP for 100 killed Undead as non-Undead.
  • Unholy Warrior: 1000 XP for 100 killed non-Undead as Undead.
  • War Criminal: 1000 XP for 100 killed enemy citizens.
  • Oil Tycoon: 1000 XP for gathering 50 000 Oil.
  • Achievement Master: 10000 XP for all completed achievements.
  • Real Estate Shark: 5000 XP for 6 purchased properties.
  • Landowner: 10000 XP for all purchased properties.
  • Explorer: 1000 XP for every 20 newly entered zones.
  • Master Explorer: 10000 XP for newly entering all zones.
  • Racer: 2000 XP for winning all races.
Environment The environment defines the visuals of the world like the sky, ambient sounds, time of day, calendar and weather.
  • Rain automatically refills all mines with resource Water.
  • Fall increases harvesting grain.
  • "-helptime": Lists time chat commands.
  • 36 days per year.
  • 12 months per year.
  • 3 days per month.
  • 24 hours per day.
  • "-ambientsound": Resets ambient sound to Sunken Ruins.
  • "-ambientsoundashenvale": Changes ambient sound to Ashenvale.
  • "-ambientsoundlordaeronsummer": Changes ambient sound to Lordaeron Summer.
  • "-noambientsound": Disables ambient sound.
  • "-sky": Resets sky to Lordaeron Summer.
  • "-skyashenvale": Changes sky to Ashenvale.
  • "-skybarrens": Changes sky to Barrens.
  • "-skyblizzard": Changes sky to Blizzard.
  • "-skydalaran": Changes sky to Dalaran.
  • "-skydalaranruins": Changes sky to Dalaran Ruins.
  • "-skyfelwood": Changes sky to Felwood.
  • "-skyfogged": Changes sky to Fogged.
  • "-skygeneric": Changes sky to Generic.
  • "-skymoon": Changes sky to Moon.
  • "-seasons": Enables seasons.
  • "-noseasons": Enables seasons.
  • "-winter": Changes season to winter.
  • "-spring": Changes season to spring.
  • "-summer": Changes season to summer.
  • "-fall": Changes season to fall.
  • "-weather": Starts weather immediately.
  • "-noweather": Stops weather immediately.
  • "-morning": Changes time of day to 6.
  • "-noon/-day": Changes time of day to 12.
  • "-evening": Changes time of day to 18.
  • "-midnight/-night": Changes time of day to 24.
  • "-dnc": Enables day and night cycle.
  • "-nodnc": Disables day and night cycle.
  • "-water"/"-nowater": Enables/disables visibility of water.
  • "-waterred": Changes the color of water to red.
  • "-fog"/"-nofog": Enables/disables visibility of fog.
  • "-reveal"/"-noreveal": Enables/disables complete map visibility.
Taunts Taunts can be used to send sounds with chat commands to other players.
  • '-taunts': Lists all taunts.
  • '-tauntson/off': Enables/disables taunts.
  • "1": Yes my lord!
  • "2": Work work!
  • "3": That's it, I am dead!
  • "4": Intriguing!
  • "5": For Lordaeron!
  • "6": I should have been a farmer like my father wanted!
  • "7": Who dares to defile this ancient land?
  • "8": Tremble mortals and despair, doom has come to this world!
  • "9": For the Alliance!
  • "10": For the Horde!
Skins Skins determine the visuals and sounds of units and buildings. They can be customized for certain units and buildings. The unit or building still is the same after changing its skin. Skins can be restricted to certain accounts or VIPs. Skin buildings allow changing skins.
  • Change visuals and sounds for units, heroes and buildings.
  • Works only for certain units, heroes and buildings.
  • Certain skins are restricted to account names.
  • Hero standard abilities allow changing skins.
  • Skin buildings allow changing skins.
  • Skin buildings can be constructed by citizens.

  • Fix automatic pick stuff in the beginning of the game to allow an instant start.

1.3 All changes of 1.3.
  • Heldenwahlansicht gefixt.

  • Texte bei Heldenauswahl korrigiert.
  • Naga-Bürger und -Bürgerinnen können über das Wasser laufen.
  • Naga können einen Laden errichten. Der Laden verkauft sogar einen winzigen Flutwächter.
  • Leben von Bäumen auf 5000.00 erhöht, damit andere Völker als die Nachtelfen länger an einer Stelle Holz sammeln können.
  • Der Völkergegenstand kann abgelegt werden. Er wird beim Repick entfernt.
  • Tempel der Gezeiten gilt als Niveau-3-Halle.
  • Spielinfos überarbeitet.
  • Irrwische sammeln 10 Holz pro Intervall, da die Bäume für andere Völker jetzt länger halten.
  • Die Essensstufen sind jetzt bei 100 und 200 weil die maximale Nahrung 300 ist.
  • Femdland-Bereich verbessert, kann jetzt jederzeit betreten werden und ermöglicht den Kauf von Dämonen.
  • Fremdland-Boss hinzugefügt.
  • Halbgötter haben auch Reittierfähigkeiten, da sonst ein Slot frei wäre.
  • Avatare der Rache beschwören wieder Rachegeister.
  • Dämonen als neues Volk hinzugefügt.
  • Ausgebildete Einheiten (mit Ausnahme der Naga) verursachen keinen Chaos-Schaden mehr.
  • "-nowin" hat "-nodefeat" ersetzt und bedeutet nun, dass das Spiel nicht gewonnen wird, wenn der neue Fremdland-Boss getötet wurde.
  • "-nowin" ist nach Ablauf des Timers nicht mehr möglich.
  • "-repick" ist nur noch alle 30 Sekunden möglich.
  • Mehr Informationen ins Quest-Log geschrieben.
  • Massen-Teleportation hat keine zunehmende Zauberverzögerung mit erhöhter Stufe.
  • Kameragrenzen verkleinert.
